name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:2-bed Room With View
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Other
info:16 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 14, 2024
msg:Ctrip Diamond upgraded the room type for free, but did not agree to give it to a room with lake view. Instead, it gave us a balcony room on the 3rd floor of Zone B with mountain view, which was quite nice. Parking is convenient, with both ground and underground garages, and ground charging piles. We arrived at the hotel at 12 o'clock and were immediately given a room. The waiter helped us carry the luggage to the room, which was great. There are many small buildings, and the whole hotel is like a park. The green garden is very good, with birds singing and flowers blooming. The air is very good, with an artificial lake and a white sand beach, a farm, a large lawn, and a canopy. There is a small hill on the hiking trail, and there are some views along the way. We walked the Shangqing Ancient Road the next day and came back to rest for another night. The food is cheap and good, highly recommended, the breakfast is also very good, and there is 24-hour delivery.
The downside is the air conditioning. Because the room was stuffy, I turned on the air conditioner for cooling (only cooling and heating), set it to 18, and the indoor temperature was 25, but it was getting hotter and hotter, reaching 28. I called the hotel and they responded that there was no air conditioning and it was under maintenance. They said they could provide fans, but there was clearly a hot air conditioner (I didn't operate it myself, it was just unified heating), so I had to turn it off. Mosquitoes were buzzing at night, and the liquid mosquito coils were colorless and odorless and ineffective. I didn't dare to open the French door because there was no screen door, and I was afraid of more mosquitoes, so I didn't sleep well. The next day I tried the air conditioner again, and the room temperature was 26. I turned on the cooling mode, and it was 27 in a while. I hurriedly turned it off, and it returned to 26 after a while. I went to buy mosquito repellent, and mosquitoes came again at night. I immediately sprayed the mosquito repellent from head to toe, and finally fell asleep all night. So the air conditioner and mosquito problems are the only flaws.
